**?? SQL**????????????

```sql
SELECT platform, merchant_id, merchant_name,
       COUNT(*)                                                      AS orders,
       ROUND(SUM(commission_amount), 2)                              AS total,
       ROUND(SUM(CASE WHEN status='rejected' THEN commission_amount ELSE 0 END), 2) AS rejected,
       ROUND(SUM(CASE WHEN status='rejected' THEN commission_amount ELSE 0 END)
             / NULLIF(SUM(commission_amount), 0) * 100, 2)           AS rate
FROM affiliate_transactions
WHERE is_deleted = 0
  AND transaction_time >= ? AND transaction_time < ?
  [AND platform = ?]
  [AND (merchant_name LIKE ? OR merchant_id LIKE ?)]
GROUP BY platform, merchant_id, merchant_name
HAVING rate >= ?
ORDER BY rate DESC, total DESC
```

```sql
SELECT platform, merchant_id,
       MAX(merchant_name)                                           AS merchant_name,          -- B-3
       COUNT(*)                                                     AS orders,
       ROUND(SUM(commission_amount), 2)                             AS total_all,              -- B-2 ???????? pending??
       ROUND(SUM(CASE WHEN status IN ('approved','rejected')
                      THEN commission_amount ELSE 0 END), 2)        AS total_settled,          -- B-2 ????
       ROUND(SUM(CASE WHEN status = 'rejected'
                      THEN commission_amount ELSE 0 END), 2)        AS rejected,
       ROUND(SUM(CASE WHEN status = 'rejected'
                      THEN commission_amount ELSE 0 END)
             / NULLIF(SUM(CASE WHEN status IN ('approved','rejected')
                               THEN commission_amount ELSE 0 END), 0) * 100, 2) AS rate         -- B-2 ????settled
FROM affiliate_transactions
WHERE is_deleted = 0
  AND transaction_time >= ?
  AND transaction_time < DATE_ADD(?, INTERVAL 1 DAY)                                            -- B-1 ????????
  [AND platform = ?]
  [AND (merchant_name LIKE ? OR merchant_id LIKE ?)]
GROUP BY platform, merchant_id                                                                  -- B-3 ?? merchant_name
HAVING rate >= ?
ORDER BY rate DESC, total_settled DESC
```

if (!matched) {
  const domain = extractDomain(txn.merchant_url || txn.click_url || '');
  if (domain) {
    const fallback = await prisma.user_merchants.findFirst({
      where: {
        user_id: currentUserId,
        platform_connection_id: currentConnId,
        source: 'url_direct',           // ??D-B10????url_direct ??
        is_deleted: 0,
        OR: [
          { merchant_url: { contains: domain } },
          { merchant_name: { contains: domain } },
        ],
      },
    });
    if (fallback) matched = fallback;
  }
}

type UrlForm = {
  merchant_url?: string;          // ?? ??

const isUrlBlockActive = (f: UrlForm) =>
  !!(f.merchant_url && f.platform_connection_id && f.country && f.publish_site_id);

function getActiveBlock(platformMerchantId: string | null, f: UrlForm): 'platform' | 'url' | null {
  if (platformMerchantId) return 'platform';
  if (isUrlBlockActive(f)) return 'url';
  return null;  // ????????????????
}

#### 21.4.3 ?????`crm-mvp/src/components/PublishSiteSelect.tsx`

```tsx
"use client";
import { Select, Tooltip, SelectProps } from "antd";

interface Site {
  id: string | number;
  site_name: string;
  domain: string;
  verified: number;       // 0 / 1
  status: string;         // 'active' / ??
  is_deleted: number;     // 0 / 1
}

interface Props extends Omit<SelectProps, "options" | "filterOption"> {
  sites: Site[];
  // ?? Select props ????
}

export default function PublishSiteSelect({ sites, ...rest }: Props) {
  const visible = sites.filter((s) => s.is_deleted === 0);

  const options = visible.map((s) => {
    const disabled = s.verified === 0 || s.status !== "active";
    const reason =
      s.verified === 0 ? "?????? :
      s.status !== "active" ? "?????? : "";
    const label = `${s.site_name} (${s.domain})`;
    return {
      value: String(s.id),
      label,
      disabled,
      site_name: s.site_name,
      domain: s.domain,
      reason,
    };
  });

  return (
    <Select
      showSearch
      allowClear
      placeholder="????????"
      optionLabelProp="label"
      filterOption={(input, option) => {
        const kw = (input || "").toLowerCase().trim();
        if (!kw) return true;
        const name = String(option?.site_name || "").toLowerCase();
        const domain = String(option?.domain || "").toLowerCase();
        return name.includes(kw) || domain.includes(kw);
      }}
      optionRender={(opt) => {
        if (opt.data.disabled && opt.data.reason) {
          return (
            <Tooltip title={opt.data.reason} placement="right">
              <span style={{ opacity: 0.5 }}>{opt.label}</span>
            </Tooltip>
          );
        }
        return opt.label;
      }}
      options={options}
      {...rest}
    />
  );
}
```

##### R1.1 ???? `optionRender` ???????21.4.3 ??????

```tsx
import { Select, Tooltip } from "antd";
import type { SelectProps } from "antd";
import type React from "react";

type Site = {
  id: string | number;
  site_name: string;
  domain: string;
  status: string;          // 'active' | 'paused' | ...
  verified: number;        // 0 | 1
  is_deleted: number;      // 0 | 1
};
type Props = Omit<SelectProps, "options"> & { sites: Site[] };

export default function PublishSiteSelect({ sites, ...rest }: Props) {
  const visible = sites.filter((s) => s.is_deleted === 0);
  const options = visible.map((s) => {
    let disabled = false;
    let reason: string | undefined;
    if (s.verified === 0) { disabled = true; reason = "??????; }
    else if (s.status !== "active") { disabled = true; reason = "??????; }
    return {
      value: String(s.id),
      label: `${s.site_name} (${s.domain})`,
      disabled,
      reason,                                   // ?????optionRender ????
      _searchText: `${s.site_name} ${s.domain}`.toLowerCase(),
    };
  });

  return (
    <Select
      showSearch
      allowClear
      placeholder="????????"
      optionLabelProp="label"
      filterOption={(input, option) => {
        const text = (option as any)?._searchText ?? "";
        return text.includes(input.toLowerCase());
      }}
      optionRender={(option) => {
        // antd 6???????? option ??????option.data
        const disabled = (option as any).disabled as boolean | undefined;
        const reason = (option as any).reason as string | undefined;
        if (disabled && reason) {
          return (
            <Tooltip title={reason} placement="right">
              <span style={{ opacity: 0.5 }}>{option.label as React.ReactNode}</span>
            </Tooltip>
          );
        }
        return option.label as React.ReactNode;
      }}
      options={options}
      {...rest}
    />
  );
}
```

```ts
type AdSettings = {
  regionMap: Map<number, string>;        // id ??abbr?? 5 ??"US"
  statusMap: Map<number, string>;        // id ??desc ???? 1 ??"active"
  fetchedAt: number;
};

const CACHE_TTL_MS = 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000;  // 24h
const cache = new Map<string, AdSettings>();   // key = token

export async function getAdSettings(token: string): Promise<AdSettings | null> {
  const hit = cache.get(token);
  if (hit && Date.now() - hit.fetchedAt < CACHE_TTL_MS) return hit;
  // ??API??0s ????????????null????????????
  // ... ??????...
}
```

#### 28.9.4 `parseMerchants` AD ????????????

```ts
// ????fetchAllMerchants AD ????????????????Settings??
const settings = await getAdSettings(token).catch(() => null);
// ?? parseMerchants ??????settings ??

function parseAdMerchant(item, settings) {
  const mid = String(item.merchantId || "");
  const name = String(item.merchantName || "");
  const statusId = Number(item.status);
  const statusDesc = settings?.statusMap.get(statusId)?.toLowerCase() || "";
  // QA10: Settings ???????????? ????????
  const passed = !settings || ["active","approved","joined","enabled"].includes(statusDesc);
  if (!passed) {
    console.log(`[MerchantDiag] AD SKIP non-active: mid=${mid} statusId=${statusId} desc=${statusDesc}`);
    return null;
  }

  const regionIds: number[] = [
    ...(typeof item.primaryRegionId === "number" ? [item.primaryRegionId] : []),
    ...(Array.isArray(item.supportRegionIds) ? item.supportRegionIds.map(Number) : []),
  ];
  const regions = settings
    ? [...new Set(regionIds.map(id => settings.regionMap.get(id)).filter(Boolean))] as string[]
    : [];

  return {
    merchant_id: mid,
    merchant_name: name,
    category: "",
    commission_rate: String(item.baseCommission || ""),
    supported_regions: regions,
    merchant_url: String(item.website || ""),
    logo_url: String(item.logo || ""),
    campaign_link: String(item.trackingLink || ""),
    relationship_status: "joined",
    epc_30d: null,
    join_date: null,
  };
}
```

export async function getAdSettings(token: string): Promise<AdSettings | null> {
  // ... fetch ...
  const regionMap = new Map<number, string>();
  for (const r of (data.region || [])) regionMap.set(Number(r.id), String(r.abbr));
  const cmStatusMap = new Map<number, string>();
  for (const s of (data.cmStatus || [])) cmStatusMap.set(Number(s.id), String(s.desc));  // ????cmStatus ??

}

#### 28.13.2 ?? ?? ?28.4.2 + ?28.9.4?`parseMerchants` AD ????

```ts
function parseAdMerchant(item, settings) {
  const statusId = Number(item.status);
  // QA10 ???????? cmStatus id=4 "Approved" ???
  // Settings ???? fallback ?????QA9??
  const approved = settings ? statusId === 4 : true;
  if (!approved) {
    console.log(`[MerchantDiag] AD SKIP non-approved: cmId=${item.cmId} mid=${item.merchantId} statusId=${statusId}`);
    return null;
  }

  const mid = String(item.merchantId || "");
  const name = String(item.merchantName || "");
  // ??category ???????????28.12.2 ????
  const category = String(item.category || "");

  // ??supportRegionIds ???????????8.12.3 ????
  const regionIdsRaw = String(item.supportRegionIds || "");
  const regionIds = regionIdsRaw ? regionIdsRaw.split(",").map(s => Number(s.trim())).filter(n => n > 0) : [];
  if (Number(item.primaryRegionId) > 0 && !regionIds.includes(Number(item.primaryRegionId))) {
    regionIds.unshift(Number(item.primaryRegionId));
  }
  const regions = settings
    ? [...new Set(regionIds.map(id => settings.regionMap.get(id)).filter(Boolean))] as string[]
    : [];

  return {
    merchant_id: mid,
    merchant_name: name,
    category,                              // ??????
    commission_rate: String(item.baseCommission || ""),   // QA5 ??baseCommission
    supported_regions: regions,
    merchant_url: String(item.website || ""),
    logo_url: String(item.logo || ""),
    campaign_link: String(item.trackingLink || ""),       // status=4 ????
    relationship_status: "joined",                         // ????status=4 ??joined
    epc_30d: null,
    join_date: null,
    // ???????cookie_duration ??user_merchants.cookie_duration??????
    _cookie_duration: Number(item.cookieExpiryDays) || null,
  };
}
```

```ts
async create({ args, query }) {
  const existing = await baseClient.affiliate_transactions.findFirst({
    where: {
      user_id, platform, merchant_id, transaction_time,
      is_deleted: 0,
      transaction_id: { not: newTxnId },
    },
  });
  if (existing) {
    return baseClient.affiliate_transactions.update({
      where: { id: existing.id },
      data: {
        commission_amount: { increment: newComm },
        order_amount: { increment: newAmt },
      },
    });
  }
  return query(args);  // ????????create
}
```

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS ad_image_ocr_cache (
  id                BIGINT UNSIGNED AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
  image_url         VARCHAR(768) NOT NULL,
  status            ENUM('pending','processing','success','failed','permanent_failure') NOT NULL DEFAULT 'pending',
  extracted_domain  VARCHAR(255) NULL,
  raw_output        VARCHAR(512) NULL,
  tries             INT UNSIGNED NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  last_error        VARCHAR(512) NULL,
  model_used        VARCHAR(64) NULL,
  prompt_tokens     INT UNSIGNED NULL,
  completion_tokens INT UNSIGNED NULL,
  lock_at           DATETIME NULL,
  created_at        DATETIME NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  updated_at        DATETIME NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,

) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4;

```typescript
// crm-mvp/src/lib/ocr-domain.ts
const VISION_PROMPT = `???????????? example.com??????????????????????????????www?????????????? none`;

async function callVisionForDomain(imageUrl: string, model: AiModelConfig): Promise<{ raw: string; ptok?: number; ctok?: number }> {
  const url = `${model.baseUrl.replace(/\/+$/, "").replace(/\/v1$/, "")}/v1/chat/completions`;
  const body = {
    model: model.modelName,
    messages: [{
      role: "user",
      content: [
        { type: "text", text: VISION_PROMPT },
        { type: "image_url", image_url: { url: imageUrl } },
      ],
    }],
    max_tokens: 64,
    temperature: 0,
  };
  const resp = await fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers: { Authorization: `Bearer ${model.apiKey}`, "Content-Type": "application/json" },
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
    signal: AbortSignal.timeout(40_000),
  });
  // ...?? choices[0].message.content + usage
}
```

### Domain ?????? gpt-4o/haiku ???? `www.x.com/`??

```typescript
function normalizeDomain(raw: string): string | null {
  const t = raw.trim().toLowerCase()
    .replace(/^https?:\/\//, "")
    .replace(/^www\./, "")
    .replace(/\/.*$/, "")
    .replace(/[,;:]$/, "");
  if (!/^([a-z0-9-]+\.)+[a-z]{2,}$/.test(t)) return null;
  // ????????????
  const BLOCK = new Set(["google.com","googleads.com","googleadservices.com","doubleclick.net","facebook.com","instagram.com"]);
  if (BLOCK.has(t)) return null;
  return t;
}
```

#### CST ????

????process ????UTC?? CST??

```typescript
function ymdCst(unixSec: number): string {
  const d = new Date(unixSec * 1000);
  d.setUTCHours(d.getUTCHours() + 8);
  return d.toISOString().slice(0, 10);
}
```

    done++;

  }
};

#### 3.2 ?? cron ???D1 + D2 + D3??

`crm-mvp/src/app/api/cron/txn-quick-sync/route.ts` ????`fetchAllTransactions` ????

```ts
const r = await fetchAllTransactions(platform, conn.api_key!, startStr, endStr);
const now = new Date();

if (r.error) {
  // ???log + ?? + ??? status
  const newFailures = (conn.consecutive_failures ?? 0) + 1;
  const newStatus = newFailures >= 3 ? 'error' : conn.status;  // ???= 3 ????07 ????
  log(`  ${user.username} ${conn.account_name} [${platform}] ERROR (${newFailures}): ${r.error}`);
  await prisma.platform_connections.update({
    where: { id: conn.id },
    data: {
      last_sync_attempt_at: now,
      last_error: r.error.slice(0, 500),
      consecutive_failures: newFailures,
      status: newStatus,
    },
  });
  continue;
}

// ???? last_synced_at + ?? error + ???? + ?? connected
await prisma.platform_connections.update({
  where: { id: conn.id },
  data: {
    last_sync_attempt_at: now,
    last_synced_at: now,
    last_error: null,
    consecutive_failures: 0,
    status: 'connected',
  },
});
```
